126#define CYLON_BUFFER_EXTRA(2*(sizeof("\x1B[0;31m")-1) + sizeof("\x1B[0;1;31m")-1 + 2*(sizeof
("\x1B[0m")-1)) (2*(sizeof(ANSI_RED"\x1B[0;31m")-1) + sizeof(ANSI_HIGHLIGHT_RED"\x1B[0;1;31m")-1 + 2*(sizeof(ANSI_NORMAL"\x1B[0m")-1))

128static void draw_cylon(char buffer[], size_t buflen, unsigned width, unsigned pos) {
129 char *p = buffer;
130
131 assert(buflen >= CYLON_BUFFER_EXTRA + width + 1)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(buflen >= (2*(sizeof("\x1B[0;31m"
)-1) + sizeof("\x1B[0;1;31m")-1 + 2*(sizeof("\x1B[0m")-1)) + width
+ 1)),0))) log_assert_failed("buflen >= CYLON_BUFFER_EXTRA + width + 1"
, "src/core/manager.c", 131, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (0
);
132 assert(pos <= width+1)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(pos <= width+1)),0))) log_assert_failed
("pos <= width+1", "src/core/manager.c", 132, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__
); } while (0); /* 0 or width+1 mean that the center light is behind the corner */
133
134 if (pos > 1) {
135 if (pos > 2)
136 p = mempset(p, ' ', pos-2);
137 p = stpcpy(p, ANSI_RED"\x1B[0;31m");
138 *p++ = '*';
139 }
140
141 if (pos > 0 && pos <= width) {
142 p = stpcpy(p, ANSI_HIGHLIGHT_RED"\x1B[0;1;31m");
143 *p++ = '*';
144 }
145
146 p = stpcpy(p, ANSI_NORMAL"\x1B[0m");
147
148 if (pos < width) {
149 p = stpcpy(p, ANSI_RED"\x1B[0;31m");
150 *p++ = '*';
151 if (pos < width-1)
152 p = mempset(p, ' ', width-1-pos);
153 strcpy(p, ANSI_NORMAL"\x1B[0m");
154 }
155}

219static int have_ask_password(void) {
220 _cleanup_closedir___attribute__((cleanup(closedirp))) DIR *dir;
221
222 dir = opendir("/run/systemd/ask-password");
223 if (!dir) {
224 if (errno(*__errno_location ()) == ENOENT2)
225 return false0;
226 else
227 return -errno(*__errno_location ());
228 }
229
230 for (;;) {
231 struct dirent *de;
232
233 errno(*__errno_location ()) = 0;
234 de = readdir(dir);
235 if (!de && errno(*__errno_location ()) > 0)
236 return -errno(*__errno_location ());
237 if (!de)
238 return false0;
239
240 if (startswith(de->d_name, "ask."))
241 return true1;
242 }
243}

, "src/core/manager.c", 415, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (0
);
416
417 /* We make liberal use of realtime signals here. On
418 * Linux/glibc we have 30 of them (with the exception of Linux
419 * on hppa, see below), between SIGRTMIN+0 ... SIGRTMIN+30
420 * (aka SIGRTMAX). */
421
422 assert_se(sigemptyset(&mask) == 0)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(sigemptyset(&mask) == 0))
,0))) log_assert_failed("sigemptyset(&mask) == 0", "src/core/manager.c"
, 422, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (0);
423 sigset_add_many(&mask,
424 SIGCHLD17, /* Child died */
425 SIGTERM15, /* Reexecute daemon */
426 SIGHUP1, /* Reload configuration */
427 SIGUSR110, /* systemd/upstart: reconnect to D-Bus */
428 SIGUSR212, /* systemd: dump status */
429 SIGINT2, /* Kernel sends us this on control-alt-del */
430 SIGWINCH28, /* Kernel sends us this on kbrequest (alt-arrowup) */
431 SIGPWR30, /* Some kernel drivers and upsd send us this on power failure */
432
433 SIGRTMIN(__libc_current_sigrtmin ())+0, /* systemd: start default.target */
434 SIGRTMIN(__libc_current_sigrtmin ())+1, /* systemd: isolate rescue.target */
435 SIGRTMIN(__libc_current_sigrtmin ())+2, /* systemd: isolate emergency.target */
436 SIGRTMIN(__libc_current_sigrtmin ())+3, /* systemd: start halt.target */
437 SIGRTMIN(__libc_current_sigrtmin ())+4, /* systemd: start poweroff.target */
438 SIGRTMIN(__libc_current_sigrtmin ())+5, /* systemd: start reboot.target */
439 SIGRTMIN(__libc_current_sigrtmin ())+6, /* systemd: start kexec.target */
440
441 /* ... space for more special targets ... */
442
443 SIGRTMIN(__libc_current_sigrtmin ())+13, /* systemd: Immediate halt */
444 SIGRTMIN(__libc_current_sigrtmin ())+14, /* systemd: Immediate poweroff */
445 SIGRTMIN(__libc_current_sigrtmin ())+15, /* systemd: Immediate reboot */
446 SIGRTMIN(__libc_current_sigrtmin ())+16, /* systemd: Immediate kexec */
447
448 /* ... space for more immediate system state changes ... */
449
450 SIGRTMIN(__libc_current_sigrtmin ())+20, /* systemd: enable status messages */
451 SIGRTMIN(__libc_current_sigrtmin ())+21, /* systemd: disable status messages */
452 SIGRTMIN(__libc_current_sigrtmin ())+22, /* systemd: set log level to LOG_DEBUG */
453 SIGRTMIN(__libc_current_sigrtmin ())+23, /* systemd: set log level to LOG_INFO */
454 SIGRTMIN(__libc_current_sigrtmin ())+24, /* systemd: Immediate exit (--user only) */
455
456 /* .. one free signal here ... */
457
458#if !defined(__hppa64__) && !defined(__hppa__)
459 /* Apparently Linux on hppa has fewer RT
460 * signals (SIGRTMAX is SIGRTMIN+25 there),
461 * hence let's not try to make use of them
462 * here. Since these commands are accessible
463 * by different means and only really a safety
464 * net, the missing functionality on hppa
465 * shouldn't matter. */
466
467 SIGRTMIN(__libc_current_sigrtmin ())+26, /* systemd: set log target to journal-or-kmsg */
468 SIGRTMIN(__libc_current_sigrtmin ())+27, /* systemd: set log target to console */
469 SIGRTMIN(__libc_current_sigrtmin ())+28, /* systemd: set log target to kmsg */
470 SIGRTMIN(__libc_current_sigrtmin ())+29, /* systemd: set log target to syslog-or-kmsg (obsolete) */
471
472 /* ... one free signal here SIGRTMIN+30 ... */
473#endif
474 -1);
475 assert_se(sigprocmask(SIG_SETMASK, &mask, NULL) == 0)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(sigprocmask(2, &mask, ((void
*)0)) == 0)),0))) log_assert_failed("sigprocmask(SIG_SETMASK, &mask, NULL) == 0"
, "src/core/manager.c", 475, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (0
);
476
477 m->signal_fd = signalfd(-1, &mask, SFD_NONBLOCKSFD_NONBLOCK|SFD_CLOEXECSFD_CLOEXEC);
478 if (m->signal_fd < 0)
479 return -errno(*__errno_location ());
480
481 r = sd_event_add_io(m->event, &m->signal_event_source, m->signal_fd, EPOLLINEPOLLIN, manager_dispatch_signal_fd, m);
482 if (r < 0)
483 return r;
484
485 (void) sd_event_source_set_description(m->signal_event_source, "manager-signal");
486
487 /* Process signals a bit earlier than the rest of things, but
488 * later than notify_fd processing, so that the notify
489 * processing can still figure out to which process/service a
490 * message belongs, before we reap the process. */
491 r = sd_event_source_set_priority(m->signal_event_source, SD_EVENT_PRIORITY_NORMAL-5);
492 if (r < 0)
493 return r;
494
495 if (MANAGER_IS_SYSTEM(m)((m)->unit_file_scope == UNIT_FILE_SYSTEM))
496 return enable_special_signals(m);
497
498 return 0;
499}

501static void manager_clean_environment(Manager *m) {
502 assert(m)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(m)),0))) log_assert_failed("m"
, "src/core/manager.c", 502, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (0

519static int manager_default_environment(Manager *m) {
520 assert(m)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(m)),0))) log_assert_failed("m"
, "src/core/manager.c", 520, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (0
);
521
522 if (MANAGER_IS_SYSTEM(m)((m)->unit_file_scope == UNIT_FILE_SYSTEM)) {
523 /* The system manager always starts with a clean
524 * environment for its children. It does not import
525 * the kernel or the parents exported variables.
526 *
527 * The initial passed environ is untouched to keep
528 * /proc/self/environ valid; it is used for tagging
529 * the init process inside containers. */
530 m->environment = strv_new("PATH=" DEFAULT_PATH"/usr/local/sbin:/usr/local/bin:/usr/sbin:/usr/bin",
531 NULL((void*)0));
532
533 /* Import locale variables LC_*= from configuration */
534 locale_setup(&m->environment);
535 } else {
536 /* The user manager passes its own environment
537 * along to its children. */
538 m->environment = strv_copy(environ);
539 }
540
541 if (!m->environment)
542 return -ENOMEM12;
543
544 manager_clean_environment(m);
545 strv_sort(m->environment);
546
547 return 0;
548}

668static int manager_setup_notify(Manager *m) {
669 int r;
670
671 if (m->test_run)
672 return 0;
673
674 if (m->notify_fd < 0) {
675 _cleanup_close___attribute__((cleanup(closep))) int fd = -1;

677 .sa.sa_family = AF_UNIX1,

679 static const int one = 1;

684 m->notify_event_source = sd_event_source_unref(m->notify_event_source);

, 688, __func__, "Failed to allocate notification socket: %m"
) : -abs(_e); });

694 log_error("Failed to determine runtime prefix.")({ int _level = (3), _e = (0); (log_get_max_level() >= ((_level
) & 0x07)) ? log_internal(_level, _e, "src/core/manager.c"
, 694, __func__, "Failed to determine runtime prefix.") : -abs
(_e); });

696 }
697
698 m->notify_socket = strappend(e, "/systemd/notify");
699 if (!m->notify_socket)

701
702 (void) mkdir_parents_label(m->notify_socket, 0755);

706 r = bind(fd, &sa.sa, offsetof(struct sockaddr_un, sun_path)__builtin_offsetof(struct sockaddr_un, sun_path) + strlen(sa.un.sun_path));
707 if (r < 0)
708 return log_error_errno(errno, "bind(%s) failed: %m", sa.un.sun_path)({ int _level = (3), _e = ((*__errno_location ())); (log_get_max_level

759static int manager_connect_bus(Manager *m, bool_Bool reexecuting) {

);

765 return 0;

768 m->kdbus_fd >= 0 ||

776static unsigned manager_dispatch_cleanup_queue(Manager *m) {
777 Unit *u;
778 unsigned n = 0;
779
780 assert(m)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(m)),0))) log_assert_failed("m"
, "src/core/manager.c", 780, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (0
);
781
782 while ((u = m->cleanup_queue)) {
783 assert(u->in_cleanup_queue)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(u->in_cleanup_queue)),0)))
log_assert_failed("u->in_cleanup_queue", "src/core/manager.c"
, 783, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (0);
784
785 unit_free(u);
786 n++;
787 }
788
789 return n;
790}
791
792enum {
793 GC_OFFSET_IN_PATH, /* This one is on the path we were traveling */
794 GC_OFFSET_UNSURE, /* No clue */
795 GC_OFFSET_GOOD, /* We still need this unit */
796 GC_OFFSET_BAD, /* We don't need this unit anymore */
797 _GC_OFFSET_MAX
798};
799
800static void unit_gc_sweep(Unit *u, unsigned gc_marker) {
801 Iterator i;
802 Unit *other;
803 bool_Bool is_bad;
804
805 assert(u)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(u)),0))) log_assert_failed("u"
, "src/core/manager.c", 805, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (0
);
806
807 if (u->gc_marker == gc_marker + GC_OFFSET_GOOD ||
808 u->gc_marker == gc_marker + GC_OFFSET_BAD ||
809 u->gc_marker == gc_marker + GC_OFFSET_IN_PATH)
810 return;
811
812 if (u->in_cleanup_queue)
813 goto bad;
814
815 if (unit_check_gc(u))
816 goto good;
817
818 u->gc_marker = gc_marker + GC_OFFSET_IN_PATH;
819
820 is_bad = true1;
821
822 SET_FOREACH(other, u->dependencies[UNIT_REFERENCED_BY], i)for ((i) = ((Iterator) { .idx = ((2147483647 *2U +1U) - 1), .
next_key = ((void*)0) }); set_iterate((u->dependencies[UNIT_REFERENCED_BY
]), &(i), (void**)&(other)); ) {
823 unit_gc_sweep(other, gc_marker);
824
825 if (other->gc_marker == gc_marker + GC_OFFSET_GOOD)
826 goto good;
827
828 if (other->gc_marker != gc_marker + GC_OFFSET_BAD)
829 is_bad = false0;
830 }
831
832 if (is_bad)
833 goto bad;
834
835 /* We were unable to find anything out about this entry, so
836 * let's investigate it later */
837 u->gc_marker = gc_marker + GC_OFFSET_UNSURE;
838 unit_add_to_gc_queue(u);
839 return;
840
841bad:
842 /* We definitely know that this one is not useful anymore, so
843 * let's mark it for deletion */
844 u->gc_marker = gc_marker + GC_OFFSET_BAD;
845 unit_add_to_cleanup_queue(u);
846 return;
847
848good:
849 u->gc_marker = gc_marker + GC_OFFSET_GOOD;
850}
851
852static unsigned manager_dispatch_gc_queue(Manager *m) {
853 Unit *u;
854 unsigned n = 0;
855 unsigned gc_marker;
856
857 assert(m)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(m)),0))) log_assert_failed("m"
, "src/core/manager.c", 857, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (0
);
858
859 /* log_debug("Running GC..."); */
860
861 m->gc_marker += _GC_OFFSET_MAX;
862 if (m->gc_marker + _GC_OFFSET_MAX <= _GC_OFFSET_MAX)
863 m->gc_marker = 1;
864
865 gc_marker = m->gc_marker;
866
867 while ((u = m->gc_queue)) {
868 assert(u->in_gc_queue)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(u->in_gc_queue)),0))) log_assert_failed
("u->in_gc_queue", "src/core/manager.c", 868, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__
); } while (0);
869
870 unit_gc_sweep(u, gc_marker);
871
872 LIST_REMOVE(gc_queue, m->gc_queue, u)do { typeof(*(m->gc_queue)) **_head = &(m->gc_queue
), *_item = (u); do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(_item)),0)))
log_assert_failed("_item", "src/core/manager.c", 872, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__
); } while (0); if (_item->gc_queue_next) _item->gc_queue_next
->gc_queue_prev = _item->gc_queue_prev; if (_item->gc_queue_prev
) _item->gc_queue_prev->gc_queue_next = _item->gc_queue_next
; else { do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(*_head == _item)),0)
)) log_assert_failed("*_head == _item", "src/core/manager.c",
872, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (0); *_head = _item->gc_queue_next
; } _item->gc_queue_next = _item->gc_queue_prev = ((void
*)0); } while (0);
873 u->in_gc_queue = false0;
874
875 n++;
876
877 if (u->gc_marker == gc_marker + GC_OFFSET_BAD ||
878 u->gc_marker == gc_marker + GC_OFFSET_UNSURE) {
879 if (u->id)
880 log_unit_debug(u, "Collecting.")({ Unit *_u = (u); _u ? log_object_internal(7, 0, "src/core/manager.c"
, 880, __func__, _u->manager->unit_log_field, _u->id
, "Collecting.") : log_internal(7, 0, "src/core/manager.c", 880
, __func__, "Collecting."); });
881 u->gc_marker = gc_marker + GC_OFFSET_BAD;
882 unit_add_to_cleanup_queue(u);
883 }
884 }
885
886 m->n_in_gc_queue = 0;
887
888 return n;
889}

891static void manager_clear_jobs_and_units(Manager *m) {

, 903, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (0);
904 assert(!m->dbus_job_queue)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(!m->dbus_job_queue)),0))) log_assert_failed
("!m->dbus_job_queue", "src/core/manager.c", 904, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__
); } while (0);

914
915Manager* manager_free(Manager *m) {
916 UnitType c;
917 int i;
918
919 if (!m)
920 return NULL((void*)0);
921
922 manager_clear_jobs_and_units(m);
923
924 for (c = 0; c < _UNIT_TYPE_MAX; c++)
925 if (unit_vtable[c]->shutdown)
926 unit_vtable[c]->shutdown(m);
927
928 /* If we reexecute ourselves, we keep the root cgroup
929 * around */
930 manager_shutdown_cgroup(m, m->exit_code != MANAGER_REEXECUTE);
931
932 lookup_paths_flush_generator(&m->lookup_paths);
933
934 bus_done(m);
935
936 hashmap_free(m->units);
937 hashmap_free(m->jobs);
938 hashmap_free(m->watch_pids1);
939 hashmap_free(m->watch_pids2);
940 hashmap_free(m->watch_bus);
941
942 set_free(m->startup_units);
943 set_free(m->failed_units);
944
945 sd_event_source_unref(m->signal_event_source);
946 sd_event_source_unref(m->notify_event_source);
947 sd_event_source_unref(m->time_change_event_source);
948 sd_event_source_unref(m->jobs_in_progress_event_source);
949 sd_event_source_unref(m->run_queue_event_source);
950
951 safe_close(m->signal_fd);
952 safe_close(m->notify_fd);
953 safe_close(m->time_change_fd);
954 safe_close(m->kdbus_fd);
955
956 manager_close_ask_password(m);
957
958 manager_close_idle_pipe(m);
959
960 udev_unref(m->udev);
961 sd_event_unref(m->event);
962
963 free(m->notify_socket);
964
965 lookup_paths_free(&m->lookup_paths);
966 strv_free(m->environment);
967
968 hashmap_free(m->cgroup_unit);
969 set_free_free(m->unit_path_cache);
970
971 free(m->switch_root);
972 free(m->switch_root_init);
973
974 for (i = 0; i < _RLIMIT_MAX(__RLIMIT_RTTIME+1 > __RLIMIT_NLIMITS ? __RLIMIT_RTTIME+1 :
__RLIMIT_NLIMITS); i++)
975 m->rlimit[i] = mfree(m->rlimit[i]);
976
977 assert(hashmap_isempty(m->units_requiring_mounts_for))do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(hashmap_isempty(m->units_requiring_mounts_for
))),0))) log_assert_failed("hashmap_isempty(m->units_requiring_mounts_for)"
, "src/core/manager.c", 977, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (0
);
978 hashmap_free(m->units_requiring_mounts_for);
979
980 free(m);
981 return NULL((void*)0);
982}
983
984void manager_enumerate(Manager *m) {
985 UnitType c;
986
987 assert(m)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(m)),0))) log_assert_failed("m"
, "src/core/manager.c", 987, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (0
);
988
989 /* Let's ask every type to load all units from disk/kernel
990 * that it might know */
991 for (c = 0; c < _UNIT_TYPE_MAX; c++) {
992 if (!unit_type_supported(c)) {
993 log_debug("Unit type .%s is not supported on this system.", unit_type_to_string(c))({ int _level = (7), _e = (0); (log_get_max_level() >= ((_level
) & 0x07)) ? log_internal(_level, _e, "src/core/manager.c"
, 993, __func__, "Unit type .%s is not supported on this system."
, unit_type_to_string(c)) : -abs(_e); });
994 continue;
995 }
996
997 if (!unit_vtable[c]->enumerate)
998 continue;
999
1000 unit_vtable[c]->enumerate(m);
1001 }
1002
1003 manager_dispatch_load_queue(m);
1004}

1006static void manager_coldplug(Manager *m) {
1007 Iterator i;
1008 Unit *u;

0);
1013
1014 /* Then, let's set up their initial state. */
1015 HASHMAP_FOREACH_KEY(u, k, m->units, i)for ((i) = ((Iterator) { .idx = ((2147483647 *2U +1U) - 1), .
next_key = ((void*)0) }); hashmap_iterate((m->units), &
(i), (void**)&(u), (const void**) &(k)); ) {
1016
1017 /* ignore aliases */

1019 continue;
1020
1021 r = unit_coldplug(u);
1022 if (r < 0)
1023 log_warning_errno(r, "We couldn't coldplug %s, proceeding anyway: %m", u->id)({ int _level = (4), _e = (r); (log_get_max_level() >= ((_level
) & 0x07)) ? log_internal(_level, _e, "src/core/manager.c"
, 1023, __func__, "We couldn't coldplug %s, proceeding anyway: %m"
, u->id) : -abs(_e); });

1027static void manager_build_unit_path_cache(Manager *m) {
1028 char **i;
1029 int r;
1030
1031 assert(m)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(m)),0))) log_assert_failed("m"
, "src/core/manager.c", 1031, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (
0);
1032

1035 m->unit_path_cache = set_new(&string_hash_ops)internal_set_new(&string_hash_ops );
1036 if (!m->unit_path_cache) {
1037 r = -ENOMEM12;
1038 goto fail;
1039 }
1040

1042 * we don't always have to go to disk */
1043
1044 STRV_FOREACH(i, m->lookup_paths.search_path)for ((i) = (m->lookup_paths.search_path); (i) && *
(i); (i)++) {

1051 log_warning_errno(errno, "Failed to open directory %s, ignoring: %m", *i)({ int _level = (4), _e = ((*__errno_location ())); (log_get_max_level
() >= ((_level) & 0x07)) ? log_internal(_level, _e, "src/core/manager.c"
, 1051, __func__, "Failed to open directory %s, ignoring: %m"
, *i) : -abs(_e); });
1052 continue;
1053 }
1054
1055 FOREACH_DIRENT(de, d, r = -errno; goto fail)for ((*__errno_location ()) = 0, de = readdir(d);; (*__errno_location
()) = 0, de = readdir(d)) if (!de) { if ((*__errno_location (
)) > 0) { r = -(*__errno_location ()); goto fail; } break;
} else if (hidden_or_backup_file((de)->d_name)) continue;
else {

1057

1062 }

) : -abs(_e); });

1077static void manager_distribute_fds(Manager *m, FDSet *fds) {
1078 Iterator i;
1079 Unit *u;
1080
1081 assert(m)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(m)),0))) log_assert_failed("m"
, "src/core/manager.c", 1081, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (
0);
1082
1083 HASHMAP_FOREACH(u, m->units, i)for ((i) = ((Iterator) { .idx = ((2147483647 *2U +1U) - 1), .
next_key = ((void*)0) }); hashmap_iterate((m->units), &
(i), (void**)&(u), ((void*)0)); ) {
1084
1085 if (fdset_size(fds) <= 0)
1086 break;
1087
1088 if (!UNIT_VTABLE(u)unit_vtable[(u)->type]->distribute_fds)
1089 continue;
1090
1091 UNIT_VTABLE(u)unit_vtable[(u)->type]->distribute_fds(u, fds);
1092 }

1094
1095int manager_startup(Manager *m, FILE *serialization, FDSet *fds) {
1096 int r, q;
1097
1098 assert(m)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(m)),0))) log_assert_failed("m"
, "src/core/manager.c", 1098, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (
0);
1099
1100 r = lookup_paths_init(&m->lookup_paths, m->unit_file_scope, 0, NULL((void*)0));
1101 if (r < 0)
1102 return r;
1103
1104 /* Make sure the transient directory always exists, so that it remains in the search path */
1105 r = mkdir_p_label(m->lookup_paths.transient, 0755);
1106 if (r < 0)
1107 return r;
1108
1109 dual_timestamp_get(&m->generators_start_timestamp);
1110 r = manager_run_generators(m);
1111 dual_timestamp_get(&m->generators_finish_timestamp);
1112 if (r < 0)
1113 return r;
1114
1115 lookup_paths_reduce(&m->lookup_paths);
1116 manager_build_unit_path_cache(m);
1117
1118 /* If we will deserialize make sure that during enumeration
1119 * this is already known, so we increase the counter here
1120 * already */
1121 if (serialization)
1122 m->n_reloading++;
1123
1124 /* First, enumerate what we can from all config files */
1125 dual_timestamp_get(&m->units_load_start_timestamp);
1126 manager_enumerate(m);
1127 dual_timestamp_get(&m->units_load_finish_timestamp);
1128
1129 /* Second, deserialize if there is something to deserialize */
1130 if (serialization)
1131 r = manager_deserialize(m, serialization, fds);
1132
1133 /* Any fds left? Find some unit which wants them. This is
1134 * useful to allow container managers to pass some file
1135 * descriptors to us pre-initialized. This enables
1136 * socket-based activation of entire containers. */
1137 manager_distribute_fds(m, fds);
1138
1139 /* We might have deserialized the notify fd, but if we didn't
1140 * then let's create the bus now */
1141 q = manager_setup_notify(m);
1142 if (q < 0 && r == 0)
1143 r = q;
1144
1145 /* We might have deserialized the kdbus control fd, but if we
1146 * didn't, then let's create the bus now. */
1147 manager_setup_kdbus(m);
1148 manager_connect_bus(m, !!serialization);
1149 bus_track_coldplug(m, &m->subscribed, &m->deserialized_subscribed);
1150
1151 /* Third, fire things up! */
1152 manager_coldplug(m);
1153
1154 if (serialization) {
1155 assert(m->n_reloading > 0)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(m->n_reloading > 0)),0)
)) log_assert_failed("m->n_reloading > 0", "src/core/manager.c"
, 1155, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (0);
1156 m->n_reloading--;
1157
1158 /* Let's wait for the UnitNew/JobNew messages being
1159 * sent, before we notify that the reload is
1160 * finished */
1161 m->send_reloading_done = true1;
1162 }
1163
1164 return r;
1165}
1166
1167int manager_add_job(Manager *m, JobType type, Unit *unit, JobMode mode, sd_bus_error *e, Job **_ret) {
1168 int r;
1169 Transaction *tr;
1170
1171 assert(m)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(m)),0))) log_assert_failed("m"
, "src/core/manager.c", 1171, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (
0);
1172 assert(type < _JOB_TYPE_MAX)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(type < _JOB_TYPE_MAX)),0))
) log_assert_failed("type < _JOB_TYPE_MAX", "src/core/manager.c"
, 1172, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (0);
1173 assert(unit)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(unit)),0))) log_assert_failed
("unit", "src/core/manager.c", 1173, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while
(0);
1174 assert(mode < _JOB_MODE_MAX)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(mode < _JOB_MODE_MAX)),0))
) log_assert_failed("mode < _JOB_MODE_MAX", "src/core/manager.c"
, 1174, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (0);
1175
1176 if (mode == JOB_ISOLATE && type != JOB_START)
1177 return sd_bus_error_setf(e, SD_BUS_ERROR_INVALID_ARGS"org.freedesktop.DBus.Error.InvalidArgs", "Isolate is only valid for start.");
1178
1179 if (mode == JOB_ISOLATE && !unit->allow_isolate)
1180 return sd_bus_error_setf(e, BUS_ERROR_NO_ISOLATION"org.freedesktop.systemd1.NoIsolation", "Operation refused, unit may not be isolated.");
1181
1182 log_unit_debug(unit, "Trying to enqueue job %s/%s/%s", unit->id, job_type_to_string(type), job_mode_to_string(mode))({ Unit *_u = (unit); _u ? log_object_internal(7, 0, "src/core/manager.c"
, 1182, __func__, _u->manager->unit_log_field, _u->id
, "Trying to enqueue job %s/%s/%s", unit->id, job_type_to_string
(type), job_mode_to_string(mode)) : log_internal(7, 0, "src/core/manager.c"
, 1182, __func__, "Trying to enqueue job %s/%s/%s", unit->
id, job_type_to_string(type), job_mode_to_string(mode)); });
1183
1184 type = job_type_collapse(type, unit);
1185
1186 tr = transaction_new(mode == JOB_REPLACE_IRREVERSIBLY);
1187 if (!tr)
1188 return -ENOMEM12;
1189
1190 r = transaction_add_job_and_dependencies(tr, type, unit, NULL((void*)0), true1, false0,
1191 mode == JOB_IGNORE_DEPENDENCIES || mode == JOB_IGNORE_REQUIREMENTS,
1192 mode == JOB_IGNORE_DEPENDENCIES, e);
1193 if (r < 0)
1194 goto tr_abort;
1195
1196 if (mode == JOB_ISOLATE) {
1197 r = transaction_add_isolate_jobs(tr, m);
1198 if (r < 0)
1199 goto tr_abort;
1200 }
1201
1202 r = transaction_activate(tr, m, mode, e);
1203 if (r < 0)
1204 goto tr_abort;
1205
1206 log_unit_debug(unit,({ Unit *_u = (unit); _u ? log_object_internal(7, 0, "src/core/manager.c"
, 1208, __func__, _u->manager->unit_log_field, _u->id
, "Enqueued job %s/%s as %u", unit->id, job_type_to_string
(type), (unsigned) tr->anchor_job->id) : log_internal(7
, 0, "src/core/manager.c", 1208, __func__, "Enqueued job %s/%s as %u"
, unit->id, job_type_to_string(type), (unsigned) tr->anchor_job
->id); })
1207 "Enqueued job %s/%s as %u", unit->id,({ Unit *_u = (unit); _u ? log_object_internal(7, 0, "src/core/manager.c"
, 1208, __func__, _u->manager->unit_log_field, _u->id
, "Enqueued job %s/%s as %u", unit->id, job_type_to_string
(type), (unsigned) tr->anchor_job->id) : log_internal(7
, 0, "src/core/manager.c", 1208, __func__, "Enqueued job %s/%s as %u"
, unit->id, job_type_to_string(type), (unsigned) tr->anchor_job
->id); })
1208 job_type_to_string(type), (unsigned) tr->anchor_job->id)({ Unit *_u = (unit); _u ? log_object_internal(7, 0, "src/core/manager.c"
, 1208, __func__, _u->manager->unit_log_field, _u->id
, "Enqueued job %s/%s as %u", unit->id, job_type_to_string
(type), (unsigned) tr->anchor_job->id) : log_internal(7
, 0, "src/core/manager.c", 1208, __func__, "Enqueued job %s/%s as %u"
, unit->id, job_type_to_string(type), (unsigned) tr->anchor_job
->id); });
1209
1210 if (_ret)
1211 *_ret = tr->anchor_job;
1212
1213 transaction_free(tr);
1214 return 0;
1215
1216tr_abort:
1217 transaction_abort(tr);
1218 transaction_free(tr);
1219 return r;
1220}

1267unsigned manager_dispatch_load_queue(Manager *m) {
1268 Unit *u;

1271 assert(m)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(m)),0))) log_assert_failed("m"
, "src/core/manager.c", 1271, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (
0);
1272
1273 /* Make sure we are not run recursively */
1274 if (m->dispatching_load_queue)
1275 return 0;
1276
1277 m->dispatching_load_queue = true1;
1278
1279 /* Dispatches the load queue. Takes a unit from the queue and
1280 * tries to load its data until the queue is empty */
1281
1282 while ((u = m->load_queue)) {
1283 assert(u->in_load_queue)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(u->in_load_queue)),0))) log_assert_failed
("u->in_load_queue", "src/core/manager.c", 1283, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__
); } while (0);
1284
1285 unit_load(u);
1286 n++;
1287 }
1288
1289 m->dispatching_load_queue = false0;
1290 return n;
1291}
1292
1293int manager_load_unit_prepare(
1294 Manager *m,
1295 const char *name,
1296 const char *path,
1297 sd_bus_error *e,
1298 Unit **_ret) {
1299
1300 Unit *ret;
1301 UnitType t;
1302 int r;
1303
1304 assert(m)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(m)),0))) log_assert_failed("m"
, "src/core/manager.c", 1304, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (
0);
1305 assert(name || path)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(name || path)),0))) log_assert_failed
("name || path", "src/core/manager.c", 1305, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__
); } while (0);
1306
1307 /* This will prepare the unit for loading, but not actually
1308 * load anything from disk. */
1309
1310 if (path && !is_path(path))
1311 return sd_bus_error_setf(e, SD_BUS_ERROR_INVALID_ARGS"org.freedesktop.DBus.Error.InvalidArgs", "Path %s is not absolute.", path);
1312
1313 if (!name)
1314 name = basename(path);
1315
1316 t = unit_name_to_type(name);
1317
1318 if (t == _UNIT_TYPE_INVALID || !unit_name_is_valid(name, UNIT_NAME_PLAIN|UNIT_NAME_INSTANCE)) {
1319 if (unit_name_is_valid(name, UNIT_NAME_TEMPLATE))
1320 return sd_bus_error_setf(e, SD_BUS_ERROR_INVALID_ARGS"org.freedesktop.DBus.Error.InvalidArgs", "Unit name %s is missing the instance name.", name);
1321
1322 return sd_bus_error_setf(e, SD_BUS_ERROR_INVALID_ARGS"org.freedesktop.DBus.Error.InvalidArgs", "Unit name %s is not valid.", name);
1323 }
1324
1325 ret = manager_get_unit(m, name);
1326 if (ret) {
1327 *_ret = ret;
1328 return 1;
1329 }
1330
1331 ret = unit_new(m, unit_vtable[t]->object_size);
1332 if (!ret)
1333 return -ENOMEM12;
1334
1335 if (path) {
1336 ret->fragment_path = strdup(path);
1337 if (!ret->fragment_path) {
1338 unit_free(ret);
1339 return -ENOMEM12;
1340 }
1341 }
1342
1343 r = unit_add_name(ret, name);
1344 if (r < 0) {
1345 unit_free(ret);
1346 return r;
1347 }
1348
1349 unit_add_to_load_queue(ret);
1350 unit_add_to_dbus_queue(ret);
1351 unit_add_to_gc_queue(ret);
1352
1353 if (_ret)
1354 *_ret = ret;
1355
1356 return 0;
1357}
1358
1359int manager_load_unit(
1360 Manager *m,
1361 const char *name,
1362 const char *path,
1363 sd_bus_error *e,
1364 Unit **_ret) {
1365
1366 int r;
1367
1368 assert(m)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(m)),0))) log_assert_failed("m"
, "src/core/manager.c", 1368, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (
0);
1369
1370 /* This will load the service information files, but not actually
1371 * start any services or anything. */
1372
1373 r = manager_load_unit_prepare(m, name, path, e, _ret);
1374 if (r != 0)
1375 return r;
1376
1377 manager_dispatch_load_queue(m);
1378
1379 if (_ret)
1380 *_ret = unit_follow_merge(*_ret);
1381
1382 return 0;
1383}

1419static int manager_dispatch_run_queue(sd_event_source *source, void *userdata) {
1420 Manager *m = userdata;
1421 Job *j;
1422
1423 assert(source)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(source)),0))) log_assert_failed
("source", "src/core/manager.c", 1423, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); }
while (0);
1424 assert(m)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(m)),0))) log_assert_failed("m"
, "src/core/manager.c", 1424, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (
0);
1425
1426 while ((j = m->run_queue)) {
1427 assert(j->installed)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(j->installed)),0))) log_assert_failed
("j->installed", "src/core/manager.c", 1427, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__
); } while (0);
1428 assert(j->in_run_queue)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(j->in_run_queue)),0))) log_assert_failed
("j->in_run_queue", "src/core/manager.c", 1428, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__
); } while (0);
1429
1430 job_run_and_invalidate(j);
1431 }
1432
1433 if (m->n_running_jobs > 0)
1434 manager_watch_jobs_in_progress(m);
1435
1436 if (m->n_on_console > 0)
1437 manager_watch_idle_pipe(m);
1438
1439 return 1;
1440}

1442static unsigned manager_dispatch_dbus_queue(Manager *m) {
1443 Job *j;
1444 Unit *u;
1445 unsigned n = 0;
1446
1447 assert(m)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(m)),0))) log_assert_failed("m"

0);
1448

1450 return 0;
1451

); } while (0);

1458 n++;
1459 }

1462 assert(j->in_dbus_queue)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(j->in_dbus_queue)),0))) log_assert_failed
("j->in_dbus_queue", "src/core/manager.c", 1462, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__
); } while (0);
1463
1464 bus_job_send_change_signal(j);
1465 n++;
1466 }
1467
1468 m->dispatching_dbus_queue = false0;
1469
1470 if (m->send_reloading_done) {
1471 m->send_reloading_done = false0;
1472
1473 bus_manager_send_reloading(m, false0);
1474 }
1475
1476 if (m->queued_message)
1477 bus_send_queued_message(m);

1480}

: -abs(_e); });

1540 if (n < 0) {

1551 n_fds = (cmsg->cmsg_len - CMSG_LEN(0)((((sizeof (struct cmsghdr)) + sizeof (size_t) - 1) & (size_t
) ~(sizeof (size_t) - 1)) + (0))) / sizeof(int);
1552
1553 } else if (cmsg->cmsg_level == SOL_SOCKET1 &&

) ~(sizeof (size_t) - 1)) + (sizeof(struct ucred)))) {
1556
1557 ucred = (struct ucred*) CMSG_DATA(cmsg)((cmsg)->__cmsg_data);

1565 if (r < 0) {

1579 }

1584 * to avoid notifying the same one multiple times. */

1587 manager_invoke_notify_message(m, u1, ucred->pid, buf, n, fds);

1589 }

1598 if (u3 && u3 != u2 && u3 != u1) {

1624
1625static int manager_dispatch_sigchld(Manager *m) {
1626 assert(m)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(m)),0))) log_assert_failed("m"

0);
1627
1628 for (;;) {
1629 siginfo_t si = {};
1630
1631 /* First we call waitd() for a PID and do not reap the
1632 * zombie. That way we can still access /proc/$PID for
1633 * it while it is a zombie. */
1634 if (waitid(P_ALL, 0, &si, WEXITED4|WNOHANG1|WNOWAIT0x01000000) < 0) {
1635
1636 if (errno(*__errno_location ()) == ECHILD10)
1637 break;
1638
1639 if (errno(*__errno_location ()) == EINTR4)
1640 continue;
1641
1642 return -errno(*__errno_location ());
1643 }
1644
1645 if (si.si_pid_sifields._kill.si_pid <= 0)
1646 break;
1647
1648 if (si.si_code == CLD_EXITEDCLD_EXITED || si.si_code == CLD_KILLEDCLD_KILLED || si.si_code == CLD_DUMPEDCLD_DUMPED) {
1649 _cleanup_free___attribute__((cleanup(freep))) char *name = NULL((void*)0);
1650 Unit *u1, *u2, *u3;
1651
1652 get_process_comm(si.si_pid_sifields._kill.si_pid, &name);
1653

, 1660, __func__, "Child ""%" "i"" (%s) died (code=%s, status=%i/%s)"

(si.si_code), si._sifields._sigchld.si_status, strna(si.si_code
== CLD_EXITED ? exit_status_to_string(si._sifields._sigchld.
si_status, EXIT_STATUS_FULL) : signal_to_string(si._sifields.
_sigchld.si_status))) : -abs(_e); })
1655 si.si_pid, strna(name),({ int _level = (7), _e = (0); (log_get_max_level() >= ((_level
) & 0x07)) ? log_internal(_level, _e, "src/core/manager.c"
, 1660, __func__, "Child ""%" "i"" (%s) died (code=%s, status=%i/%s)"
, si._sifields._kill.si_pid, strna(name), sigchld_code_to_string
(si.si_code), si._sifields._sigchld.si_status, strna(si.si_code
== CLD_EXITED ? exit_status_to_string(si._sifields._sigchld.

1656 sigchld_code_to_string(si.si_code),({ int _level = (7), _e = (0); (log_get_max_level() >= ((_level
) & 0x07)) ? log_internal(_level, _e, "src/core/manager.c"
, 1660, __func__, "Child ""%" "i"" (%s) died (code=%s, status=%i/%s)"

== CLD_EXITED ? exit_status_to_string(si._sifields._sigchld.

_sigchld.si_status))) : -abs(_e); })
1657 si.si_status,({ int _level = (7), _e = (0); (log_get_max_level() >= ((_level
) & 0x07)) ? log_internal(_level, _e, "src/core/manager.c"
, 1660, __func__, "Child ""%" "i"" (%s) died (code=%s, status=%i/%s)"
, si._sifields._kill.si_pid, strna(name), sigchld_code_to_string
(si.si_code), si._sifields._sigchld.si_status, strna(si.si_code
== CLD_EXITED ? exit_status_to_string(si._sifields._sigchld.
si_status, EXIT_STATUS_FULL) : signal_to_string(si._sifields.
_sigchld.si_status))) : -abs(_e); })
1658 strna(si.si_code == CLD_EXITED({ int _level = (7), _e = (0); (log_get_max_level() >= ((_level
) & 0x07)) ? log_internal(_level, _e, "src/core/manager.c"
, 1660, __func__, "Child ""%" "i"" (%s) died (code=%s, status=%i/%s)"
, si._sifields._kill.si_pid, strna(name), sigchld_code_to_string
(si.si_code), si._sifields._sigchld.si_status, strna(si.si_code
== CLD_EXITED ? exit_status_to_string(si._sifields._sigchld.
si_status, EXIT_STATUS_FULL) : signal_to_string(si._sifields.
_sigchld.si_status))) : -abs(_e); })
1659 ? exit_status_to_string(si.si_status, EXIT_STATUS_FULL)({ int _level = (7), _e = (0); (log_get_max_level() >= ((_level
) & 0x07)) ? log_internal(_level, _e, "src/core/manager.c"
, 1660, __func__, "Child ""%" "i"" (%s) died (code=%s, status=%i/%s)"
, si._sifields._kill.si_pid, strna(name), sigchld_code_to_string
(si.si_code), si._sifields._sigchld.si_status, strna(si.si_code
== CLD_EXITED ? exit_status_to_string(si._sifields._sigchld.
si_status, EXIT_STATUS_FULL) : signal_to_string(si._sifields.
_sigchld.si_status))) : -abs(_e); })
1660 : signal_to_string(si.si_status)))({ int _level = (7), _e = (0); (log_get_max_level() >= ((_level
) & 0x07)) ? log_internal(_level, _e, "src/core/manager.c"
, 1660, __func__, "Child ""%" "i"" (%s) died (code=%s, status=%i/%s)"
, si._sifields._kill.si_pid, strna(name), sigchld_code_to_string
(si.si_code), si._sifields._sigchld.si_status, strna(si.si_code
== CLD_EXITED ? exit_status_to_string(si._sifields._sigchld.
si_status, EXIT_STATUS_FULL) : signal_to_string(si._sifields.
_sigchld.si_status))) : -abs(_e); });
1661
1662 /* And now figure out the unit this belongs
1663 * to, it might be multiple... */
1664 u1 = manager_get_unit_by_pid_cgroup(m, si.si_pid_sifields._kill.si_pid);
1665 if (u1)
1666 invoke_sigchld_event(m, u1, &si);
1667 u2 = hashmap_get(m->watch_pids1, PID_TO_PTR(si.si_pid)((void*) ((uintptr_t) si._sifields._kill.si_pid)));
1668 if (u2 && u2 != u1)
1669 invoke_sigchld_event(m, u2, &si);
1670 u3 = hashmap_get(m->watch_pids2, PID_TO_PTR(si.si_pid)((void*) ((uintptr_t) si._sifields._kill.si_pid)));
1671 if (u3 && u3 != u2 && u3 != u1)
1672 invoke_sigchld_event(m, u3, &si);
1673 }
1674
1675 /* And now, we actually reap the zombie. */
1676 if (waitid(P_PID, si.si_pid_sifields._kill.si_pid, &si, WEXITED4) < 0) {
1677 if (errno(*__errno_location ()) == EINTR4)
1678 continue;
1679
1680 return -errno(*__errno_location ());
1681 }
1682 }
1683
1684 return 0;
1685}

1687static int manager_start_target(Manager *m, const char *name, JobMode mode) {
1688 _cleanup_(sd_bus_error_free)__attribute__((cleanup(sd_bus_error_free))) sd_bus_error error = SD_BUS_ERROR_NULL((const sd_bus_error) {(((void*)0)), (((void*)0)), 0});

1690
1691 log_debug("Activating special unit %s", name)({ int _level = (7), _e = (0); (log_get_max_level() >= ((_level
) & 0x07)) ? log_internal(_level, _e, "src/core/manager.c"

_e); });

1694 if (r < 0)

) & 0x07)) ? log_internal(_level, _e, "src/core/manager.c"
, 1695, __func__, "Failed to enqueue %s job: %s", name, bus_error_message

1700static int manager_dispatch_signal_fd(sd_event_source *source, int fd, uint32_t revents, void *userdata) {
1701 Manager *m = userdata;
1702 ssize_t n;
1703 struct signalfd_siginfo sfsi;
1704 bool_Bool sigchld = false0;
1705 int r;
1706
1707 assert(m)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(m)),0))) log_assert_failed("m"
, "src/core/manager.c", 1707, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (
0);
1708 assert(m->signal_fd == fd)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(m->signal_fd == fd)),0))) log_assert_failed
("m->signal_fd == fd", "src/core/manager.c", 1708, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__
); } while (0);
1709
1710 if (revents != EPOLLINEPOLLIN) {
1711 log_warning("Got unexpected events from signal file descriptor.")({ int _level = (4), _e = (0); (log_get_max_level() >= ((_level
) & 0x07)) ? log_internal(_level, _e, "src/core/manager.c"
, 1711, __func__, "Got unexpected events from signal file descriptor."
) : -abs(_e); });
1712 return 0;
1713 }
1714
1715 for (;;) {
1716 n = read(m->signal_fd, &sfsi, sizeof(sfsi));
1717 if (n != sizeof(sfsi)) {
1718
1719 if (n >= 0)
1720 return -EIO5;
1721
1722 if (errno(*__errno_location ()) == EINTR4 || errno(*__errno_location ()) == EAGAIN11)
1723 break;
1724
1725 return -errno(*__errno_location ());
1726 }
1727
1728 log_received_signal(sfsi.ssi_signo == SIGCHLD17 ||
1729 (sfsi.ssi_signo == SIGTERM15 && MANAGER_IS_USER(m)((m)->unit_file_scope != UNIT_FILE_SYSTEM))
1730 ? LOG_DEBUG7 : LOG_INFO6,
1731 &sfsi);
1732
1733 switch (sfsi.ssi_signo) {
1734
1735 case SIGCHLD17:
1736 sigchld = true1;
1737 break;
1738
1739 case SIGTERM15:
1740 if (MANAGER_IS_SYSTEM(m)((m)->unit_file_scope == UNIT_FILE_SYSTEM)) {
1741 /* This is for compatibility with the
1742 * original sysvinit */
1743 m->exit_code = MANAGER_REEXECUTE;
1744 break;
1745 }
1746
1747 /* Fall through */
1748
1749 case SIGINT2:
1750 if (MANAGER_IS_SYSTEM(m)((m)->unit_file_scope == UNIT_FILE_SYSTEM)) {
1751
1752 /* If the user presses C-A-D more than
1753 * 7 times within 2s, we reboot
1754 * immediately. */
1755
1756 if (ratelimit_test(&m->ctrl_alt_del_ratelimit))
1757 manager_start_target(m, SPECIAL_CTRL_ALT_DEL_TARGET"ctrl-alt-del.target", JOB_REPLACE_IRREVERSIBLY);
1758 else {
1759 log_notice("Ctrl-Alt-Del was pressed more than 7 times within 2s, rebooting immediately.")({ int _level = (5), _e = (0); (log_get_max_level() >= ((_level
) & 0x07)) ? log_internal(_level, _e, "src/core/manager.c"
, 1759, __func__, "Ctrl-Alt-Del was pressed more than 7 times within 2s, rebooting immediately."
) : -abs(_e); });
1760 status_printf(NULL((void*)0), true1, false0, "Ctrl-Alt-Del was pressed more than 7 times within 2s, rebooting immediately.");
1761 m->exit_code = MANAGER_REBOOT;
1762 }
1763
1764 break;
1765 }
1766
1767 /* Run the exit target if there is one, if not, just exit. */
1768 if (manager_start_target(m, SPECIAL_EXIT_TARGET"exit.target", JOB_REPLACE) < 0) {
1769 m->exit_code = MANAGER_EXIT;
1770 return 0;
1771 }
1772
1773 break;
1774
1775 case SIGWINCH28:
1776 if (MANAGER_IS_SYSTEM(m)((m)->unit_file_scope == UNIT_FILE_SYSTEM))
1777 manager_start_target(m, SPECIAL_KBREQUEST_TARGET"kbrequest.target", JOB_REPLACE);
1778
1779 /* This is a nop on non-init */
1780 break;
1781
1782 case SIGPWR30:
1783 if (MANAGER_IS_SYSTEM(m)((m)->unit_file_scope == UNIT_FILE_SYSTEM))
1784 manager_start_target(m, SPECIAL_SIGPWR_TARGET"sigpwr.target", JOB_REPLACE);
1785
1786 /* This is a nop on non-init */
1787 break;
1788
1789 case SIGUSR110: {
1790 Unit *u;
1791
1792 u = manager_get_unit(m, SPECIAL_DBUS_SERVICE"dbus.service");
1793
1794 if (!u || UNIT_IS_ACTIVE_OR_RELOADING(unit_active_state(u))) {
1795 log_info("Trying to reconnect to bus...")({ int _level = (6), _e = (0); (log_get_max_level() >= ((_level
) & 0x07)) ? log_internal(_level, _e, "src/core/manager.c"
, 1795, __func__, "Trying to reconnect to bus...") : -abs(_e)
; });
1796 bus_init(m, true1);
1797 }
1798
1799 if (!u || !UNIT_IS_ACTIVE_OR_ACTIVATING(unit_active_state(u))) {
1800 log_info("Loading D-Bus service...")({ int _level = (6), _e = (0); (log_get_max_level() >= ((_level
) & 0x07)) ? log_internal(_level, _e, "src/core/manager.c"
, 1800, __func__, "Loading D-Bus service...") : -abs(_e); });
1801 manager_start_target(m, SPECIAL_DBUS_SERVICE"dbus.service", JOB_REPLACE);
1802 }
1803
1804 break;
1805 }
1806
1807 case SIGUSR212: {
1808 _cleanup_free___attribute__((cleanup(freep))) char *dump = NULL((void*)0);
1809 _cleanup_fclose___attribute__((cleanup(fclosep))) FILE *f = NULL((void*)0);
1810 size_t size;
1811
1812 f = open_memstream(&dump, &size);
1813 if (!f) {
1814 log_warning_errno(errno, "Failed to allocate memory stream: %m")({ int _level = (4), _e = ((*__errno_location ())); (log_get_max_level
() >= ((_level) & 0x07)) ? log_internal(_level, _e, "src/core/manager.c"
, 1814, __func__, "Failed to allocate memory stream: %m") : -
abs(_e); });
1815 break;
1816 }
1817
1818 manager_dump_units(m, f, "\t");
1819 manager_dump_jobs(m, f, "\t");
1820
1821 r = fflush_and_check(f);
1822 if (r < 0) {
1823 log_warning_errno(r, "Failed to write status stream: %m")({ int _level = (4), _e = (r); (log_get_max_level() >= ((_level
) & 0x07)) ? log_internal(_level, _e, "src/core/manager.c"
, 1823, __func__, "Failed to write status stream: %m") : -abs
(_e); });
1824 break;
1825 }
1826
1827 log_dump(LOG_INFO, dump)log_dump_internal(6, 0, "src/core/manager.c", 1827, __func__,
dump);
1828 break;
1829 }
1830
1831 case SIGHUP1:
1832 m->exit_code = MANAGER_RELOAD;
1833 break;
1834
1835 default: {
1836
1837 /* Starting SIGRTMIN+0 */
1838 static const char * const target_table[] = {
1839 [0] = SPECIAL_DEFAULT_TARGET"default.target",
1840 [1] = SPECIAL_RESCUE_TARGET"rescue.target",
1841 [2] = SPECIAL_EMERGENCY_TARGET"emergency.target",
1842 [3] = SPECIAL_HALT_TARGET"halt.target",
1843 [4] = SPECIAL_POWEROFF_TARGET"poweroff.target",
1844 [5] = SPECIAL_REBOOT_TARGET"reboot.target",
1845 [6] = SPECIAL_KEXEC_TARGET"kexec.target"
1846 };
1847
1848 /* Starting SIGRTMIN+13, so that target halt and system halt are 10 apart */
1849 static const ManagerExitCode code_table[] = {
1850 [0] = MANAGER_HALT,
1851 [1] = MANAGER_POWEROFF,
1852 [2] = MANAGER_REBOOT,
1853 [3] = MANAGER_KEXEC
1854 };
1855
1856 if ((int) sfsi.ssi_signo >= SIGRTMIN(__libc_current_sigrtmin ())+0 &&
1857 (int) sfsi.ssi_signo < SIGRTMIN(__libc_current_sigrtmin ())+(int) ELEMENTSOF(target_table)__extension__ (__builtin_choose_expr( !__builtin_types_compatible_p
(typeof(target_table), typeof(&*(target_table))), sizeof(
target_table)/sizeof((target_table)[0]), (void)0))) {
1858 int idx = (int) sfsi.ssi_signo - SIGRTMIN(__libc_current_sigrtmin ());
1859 manager_start_target(m, target_table[idx],
1860 (idx == 1 || idx == 2) ? JOB_ISOLATE : JOB_REPLACE);
1861 break;
1862 }
1863
1864 if ((int) sfsi.ssi_signo >= SIGRTMIN(__libc_current_sigrtmin ())+13 &&
1865 (int) sfsi.ssi_signo < SIGRTMIN(__libc_current_sigrtmin ())+13+(int) ELEMENTSOF(code_table)__extension__ (__builtin_choose_expr( !__builtin_types_compatible_p
(typeof(code_table), typeof(&*(code_table))), sizeof(code_table
)/sizeof((code_table)[0]), (void)0))) {
1866 m->exit_code = code_table[sfsi.ssi_signo - SIGRTMIN(__libc_current_sigrtmin ()) - 13];
1867 break;
1868 }
1869
1870 switch (sfsi.ssi_signo - SIGRTMIN(__libc_current_sigrtmin ())) {
1871
1872 case 20:
1873 manager_set_show_status(m, SHOW_STATUS_YES);
1874 break;
1875
1876 case 21:
1877 manager_set_show_status(m, SHOW_STATUS_NO);
1878 break;
1879
1880 case 22:
1881 log_set_max_level(LOG_DEBUG7);
1882 log_info("Setting log level to debug.")({ int _level = (6), _e = (0); (log_get_max_level() >= ((_level
) & 0x07)) ? log_internal(_level, _e, "src/core/manager.c"
, 1882, __func__, "Setting log level to debug.") : -abs(_e); }
);
1883 break;
1884
1885 case 23:
1886 log_set_max_level(LOG_INFO6);
1887 log_info("Setting log level to info.")({ int _level = (6), _e = (0); (log_get_max_level() >= ((_level
) & 0x07)) ? log_internal(_level, _e, "src/core/manager.c"
, 1887, __func__, "Setting log level to info.") : -abs(_e); }
);
1888 break;
1889
1890 case 24:
1891 if (MANAGER_IS_USER(m)((m)->unit_file_scope != UNIT_FILE_SYSTEM)) {
1892 m->exit_code = MANAGER_EXIT;
1893 return 0;
1894 }
1895
1896 /* This is a nop on init */
1897 break;
1898
1899 case 26:
1900 case 29: /* compatibility: used to be mapped to LOG_TARGET_SYSLOG_OR_KMSG */
1901 log_set_target(LOG_TARGET_JOURNAL_OR_KMSG);
1902 log_notice("Setting log target to journal-or-kmsg.")({ int _level = (5), _e = (0); (log_get_max_level() >= ((_level
) & 0x07)) ? log_internal(_level, _e, "src/core/manager.c"
, 1902, __func__, "Setting log target to journal-or-kmsg.") :
-abs(_e); });
1903 break;
1904
1905 case 27:
1906 log_set_target(LOG_TARGET_CONSOLE);
1907 log_notice("Setting log target to console.")({ int _level = (5), _e = (0); (log_get_max_level() >= ((_level
) & 0x07)) ? log_internal(_level, _e, "src/core/manager.c"
, 1907, __func__, "Setting log target to console.") : -abs(_e
); });
1908 break;
1909
1910 case 28:
1911 log_set_target(LOG_TARGET_KMSG);
1912 log_notice("Setting log target to kmsg.")({ int _level = (5), _e = (0); (log_get_max_level() >= ((_level
) & 0x07)) ? log_internal(_level, _e, "src/core/manager.c"
, 1912, __func__, "Setting log target to kmsg.") : -abs(_e); }
);
1913 break;
1914
1915 default:
1916 log_warning("Got unhandled signal <%s>.", signal_to_string(sfsi.ssi_signo))({ int _level = (4), _e = (0); (log_get_max_level() >= ((_level
) & 0x07)) ? log_internal(_level, _e, "src/core/manager.c"
, 1916, __func__, "Got unhandled signal <%s>.", signal_to_string
(sfsi.ssi_signo)) : -abs(_e); });
1917 }
1918 }
1919 }
1920 }
1921
1922 if (sigchld)
1923 manager_dispatch_sigchld(m);
1924
1925 return 0;
1926}

1985int manager_loop(Manager *m) {
1986 int r;
1987
1988 RATELIMIT_DEFINE(rl, 1*USEC_PER_SEC, 50000)RateLimit rl = { .interval = (1*((usec_t) 1000000ULL)), .burst
= (50000), .num = 0, .begin = 0 };
1989
1990 assert(m)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(m)),0))) log_assert_failed("m"
, "src/core/manager.c", 1990, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (
0);
1991 m->exit_code = MANAGER_OK;
1992
1993 /* Release the path cache */
1994 m->unit_path_cache = set_free_free(m->unit_path_cache);
1995
1996 manager_check_finished(m);
1997
1998 /* There might still be some zombies hanging around from
1999 * before we were exec()'ed. Let's reap them. */
2000 r = manager_dispatch_sigchld(m);
2001 if (r < 0)
2002 return r;
2003
2004 while (m->exit_code == MANAGER_OK) {
2005 usec_t wait_usec;
2006
2007 if (m->runtime_watchdog > 0 && m->runtime_watchdog != USEC_INFINITY((usec_t) -1) && MANAGER_IS_SYSTEM(m)((m)->unit_file_scope == UNIT_FILE_SYSTEM))
2008 watchdog_ping();
2009
2010 if (!ratelimit_test(&rl)) {
2011 /* Yay, something is going seriously wrong, pause a little */
2012 log_warning("Looping too fast. Throttling execution a little.")({ int _level = (4), _e = (0); (log_get_max_level() >= ((_level
) & 0x07)) ? log_internal(_level, _e, "src/core/manager.c"
, 2012, __func__, "Looping too fast. Throttling execution a little."
) : -abs(_e); });
2013 sleep(1);
2014 }
2015
2016 if (manager_dispatch_load_queue(m) > 0)
2017 continue;
2018
2019 if (manager_dispatch_gc_queue(m) > 0)
2020 continue;
2021
2022 if (manager_dispatch_cleanup_queue(m) > 0)
2023 continue;
2024
2025 if (manager_dispatch_cgroup_queue(m) > 0)
2026 continue;
2027
2028 if (manager_dispatch_dbus_queue(m) > 0)
2029 continue;
2030
2031 /* Sleep for half the watchdog time */
2032 if (m->runtime_watchdog > 0 && m->runtime_watchdog != USEC_INFINITY((usec_t) -1) && MANAGER_IS_SYSTEM(m)((m)->unit_file_scope == UNIT_FILE_SYSTEM)) {
2033 wait_usec = m->runtime_watchdog / 2;
2034 if (wait_usec <= 0)
2035 wait_usec = 1;
2036 } else
2037 wait_usec = USEC_INFINITY((usec_t) -1);
2038
2039 r = sd_event_run(m->event, wait_usec);
2040 if (r < 0)
2041 return log_error_errno(r, "Failed to run event loop: %m")({ int _level = (3), _e = (r); (log_get_max_level() >= ((_level
) & 0x07)) ? log_internal(_level, _e, "src/core/manager.c"
, 2041, __func__, "Failed to run event loop: %m") : -abs(_e);
});
2042 }
2043
2044 return m->exit_code;
2045}

2137void manager_send_unit_plymouth(Manager *m, Unit *u) {
2138 union sockaddr_union sa = PLYMOUTH_SOCKET{ .un.sun_family = 1, .un.sun_path = "\0/org/freedesktop/plymouthd"

2144 /* Don't generate plymouth events if the service was already
2145 * started and we're just deserializing */

2491int manager_reload(Manager *m) {
2492 int r, q;
2493 _cleanup_fclose___attribute__((cleanup(fclosep))) FILE *f = NULL((void*)0);
2494 _cleanup_fdset_free___attribute__((cleanup(fdset_freep))) FDSet *fds = NULL((void*)0);
2495
2496 assert(m)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(m)),0))) log_assert_failed("m"
, "src/core/manager.c", 2496, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (
0);
2497
2498 r = manager_open_serialization(m, &f);
2499 if (r < 0)
2500 return r;
2501
2502 m->n_reloading++;
2503 bus_manager_send_reloading(m, true1);
2504
2505 fds = fdset_new();
2506 if (!fds) {
2507 m->n_reloading--;
2508 return -ENOMEM12;
2509 }
2510
2511 r = manager_serialize(m, f, fds, false0);
2512 if (r < 0) {
2513 m->n_reloading--;
2514 return r;
2515 }
2516
2517 if (fseeko(f, 0, SEEK_SET0) < 0) {
2518 m->n_reloading--;
2519 return -errno(*__errno_location ());
2520 }
2521
2522 /* From here on there is no way back. */
2523 manager_clear_jobs_and_units(m);
2524 lookup_paths_flush_generator(&m->lookup_paths);
2525 lookup_paths_free(&m->lookup_paths);
2526
2527 q = lookup_paths_init(&m->lookup_paths, m->unit_file_scope, 0, NULL((void*)0));
2528 if (q < 0 && r >= 0)
2529 r = q;
2530
2531 /* Find new unit paths */
2532 q = manager_run_generators(m);
2533 if (q < 0 && r >= 0)
2534 r = q;
2535
2536 lookup_paths_reduce(&m->lookup_paths);
2537 manager_build_unit_path_cache(m);
2538
2539 /* First, enumerate what we can from all config files */
2540 manager_enumerate(m);
2541
2542 /* Second, deserialize our stored data */
2543 q = manager_deserialize(m, f, fds);
2544 if (q < 0 && r >= 0)
2545 r = q;
2546
2547 fclose(f);
2548 f = NULL((void*)0);
2549
2550 /* Re-register notify_fd as event source */
2551 q = manager_setup_notify(m);
2552 if (q < 0 && r >= 0)
2553 r = q;
2554
2555 /* Third, fire things up! */
2556 manager_coldplug(m);
2557
2558 /* Sync current state of bus names with our set of listening units */
2559 if (m->api_bus)
2560 manager_sync_bus_names(m, m->api_bus);
2561
2562 assert(m->n_reloading > 0)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(m->n_reloading > 0)),0)
)) log_assert_failed("m->n_reloading > 0", "src/core/manager.c"
, 2562, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (0);
2563 m->n_reloading--;
2564
2565 m->send_reloading_done = true1;
2566
2567 return r;
2568}

2594static void manager_notify_finished(Manager *m) {
2595 char userspace[FORMAT_TIMESPAN_MAX64], initrd[FORMAT_TIMESPAN_MAX64], kernel[FORMAT_TIMESPAN_MAX64], sum[FORMAT_TIMESPAN_MAX64];
2596 usec_t firmware_usec, loader_usec, kernel_usec, initrd_usec, userspace_usec, total_usec;
2597
2598 if (m->test_run)
2599 return;
2600
2601 if (MANAGER_IS_SYSTEM(m)((m)->unit_file_scope == UNIT_FILE_SYSTEM) && detect_container() <= 0) {
2602
2603 /* Note that m->kernel_usec.monotonic is always at 0,
2604 * and m->firmware_usec.monotonic and
2605 * m->loader_usec.monotonic should be considered
2606 * negative values. */
2607
2608 firmware_usec = m->firmware_timestamp.monotonic - m->loader_timestamp.monotonic;
2609 loader_usec = m->loader_timestamp.monotonic - m->kernel_timestamp.monotonic;
2610 userspace_usec = m->finish_timestamp.monotonic - m->userspace_timestamp.monotonic;
2611 total_usec = m->firmware_timestamp.monotonic + m->finish_timestamp.monotonic;
2612
2613 if (dual_timestamp_is_set(&m->initrd_timestamp)) {
2614
2615 kernel_usec = m->initrd_timestamp.monotonic - m->kernel_timestamp.monotonic;

2662
2663void manager_check_finished(Manager *m) {
2664 assert(m)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(m)),0))) log_assert_failed("m"
, "src/core/manager.c", 2664, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (
0);
2665
2666 if (MANAGER_IS_RELOADING(m)((m)->n_reloading > 0))
2667 return;
2668
2669 /* Verify that we are actually running currently. Initially
2670 * the exit code is set to invalid, and during operation it is
2671 * then set to MANAGER_OK */
2672 if (m->exit_code != MANAGER_OK)
2673 return;
2674
2675 if (hashmap_size(m->jobs) > 0) {
2676 if (m->jobs_in_progress_event_source)
2677 /* Ignore any failure, this is only for feedback */
2678 (void) sd_event_source_set_time(m->jobs_in_progress_event_source, now(CLOCK_MONOTONIC1) + JOBS_IN_PROGRESS_WAIT_USEC(5*((usec_t) 1000000ULL)));
2679
2680 return;
2681 }
2682
2683 manager_flip_auto_status(m, false0);
2684
2685 /* Notify Type=idle units that we are done now */
2686 manager_close_idle_pipe(m);
2687
2688 /* Turn off confirm spawn now */
2689 m->confirm_spawn = false0;
2690
2691 /* No need to update ask password status when we're going non-interactive */
2692 manager_close_ask_password(m);
2693
2694 /* This is no longer the first boot */
2695 manager_set_first_boot(m, false0);
2696
2697 if (dual_timestamp_is_set(&m->finish_timestamp))
2698 return;
2699
2700 dual_timestamp_get(&m->finish_timestamp);
2701
2702 manager_notify_finished(m);
2703
2704 manager_invalidate_startup_units(m);
2705}

2707static int manager_run_generators(Manager *m) {
2708 _cleanup_strv_free___attribute__((cleanup(strv_freep))) char **paths = NULL((void*)0);
2709 const char *argv[5];
2710 char **path;
2711 int r;
2712
2713 assert(m)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(m)),0))) log_assert_failed("m"
, "src/core/manager.c", 2713, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (
0);
2714
2715 if (m->test_run)
2716 return 0;
2717
2718 paths = generator_binary_paths(m->unit_file_scope);
2719 if (!paths)
2720 return log_oom()log_oom_internal("src/core/manager.c", 2720, __func__);
2721
2722 /* Optimize by skipping the whole process by not creating output directories
2723 * if no generators are found. */
2724 STRV_FOREACH(path, paths)for ((path) = (paths); (path) && *(path); (path)++) {
2725 if (access(*path, F_OK0) >= 0)
2726 goto found;
2727 if (errno(*__errno_location ()) != ENOENT2)
2728 log_warning_errno(errno, "Failed to open generator directory %s: %m", *path)({ int _level = (4), _e = ((*__errno_location ())); (log_get_max_level
() >= ((_level) & 0x07)) ? log_internal(_level, _e, "src/core/manager.c"
, 2728, __func__, "Failed to open generator directory %s: %m"
, *path) : -abs(_e); });
2729 }
2730
2731 return 0;
2732
2733 found:
2734 r = lookup_paths_mkdir_generator(&m->lookup_paths);
2735 if (r < 0)
2736 goto finish;
2737
2738 argv[0] = NULL((void*)0); /* Leave this empty, execute_directory() will fill something in */
2739 argv[1] = m->lookup_paths.generator;
2740 argv[2] = m->lookup_paths.generator_early;
2741 argv[3] = m->lookup_paths.generator_late;
2742 argv[4] = NULL((void*)0);
2743
2744 RUN_WITH_UMASK(0022)for (__attribute__((cleanup(_reset_umask_))) struct _umask_struct_
_saved_umask_ = { umask(0022), 0 }; !_saved_umask_.quit ; _saved_umask_
.quit = 1)
2745 execute_directories((const char* const*) paths, DEFAULT_TIMEOUT_USEC(90*((usec_t) 1000000ULL)), (char**) argv);
2746
2747finish:
2748 lookup_paths_trim_generator(&m->lookup_paths);
2749 return r;
2750}
2751
2752int manager_environment_add(Manager *m, char **minus, char **plus) {
2753 char **a = NULL((void*)0), **b = NULL((void*)0), **l;
2754 assert(m)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(m)),0))) log_assert_failed("m"
, "src/core/manager.c", 2754, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (
0);
2755
2756 l = m->environment;
2757
2758 if (!strv_isempty(minus)) {
2759 a = strv_env_delete(l, 1, minus);
2760 if (!a)
2761 return -ENOMEM12;
2762
2763 l = a;
2764 }
2765
2766 if (!strv_isempty(plus)) {
2767 b = strv_env_merge(2, l, plus);
2768 if (!b) {
2769 strv_free(a);
2770 return -ENOMEM12;
2771 }
2772
2773 l = b;
2774 }
2775
2776 if (m->environment != l)
2777 strv_free(m->environment);
2778 if (a != l)
2779 strv_free(a);
2780 if (b != l)
2781 strv_free(b);
2782
2783 m->environment = l;
2784 manager_clean_environment(m);
2785 strv_sort(m->environment);
2786
2787 return 0;
2788}

2790int manager_set_default_rlimits(Manager *m, struct rlimit **default_rlimit) {
2791 int i;
2792
2793 assert(m)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(m)),0))) log_assert_failed("m"
, "src/core/manager.c", 2793, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (
0);
2794
2795 for (i = 0; i < _RLIMIT_MAX(__RLIMIT_RTTIME+1 > __RLIMIT_NLIMITS ? __RLIMIT_RTTIME+1 :
__RLIMIT_NLIMITS); i++) {
2796 m->rlimit[i] = mfree(m->rlimit[i]);
2797
2798 if (!default_rlimit[i])
2799 continue;
2800
2801 m->rlimit[i] = newdup(struct rlimit, default_rlimit[i], 1)((struct rlimit*) memdup_multiply(default_rlimit[i], sizeof(struct
rlimit), (1)));
2802 if (!m->rlimit[i])
2803 return -ENOMEM12;
2804 }
2805
2806 return 0;
2807}
2808
2809void manager_recheck_journal(Manager *m) {
2810 Unit *u;
2811
2812 assert(m)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(m)),0))) log_assert_failed("m"
, "src/core/manager.c", 2812, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (
0);
2813
2814 if (!MANAGER_IS_SYSTEM(m)((m)->unit_file_scope == UNIT_FILE_SYSTEM))
2815 return;
2816
2817 u = manager_get_unit(m, SPECIAL_JOURNALD_SOCKET"systemd-journald.socket");
2818 if (u && SOCKET(u)->state != SOCKET_RUNNING) {
2819 log_close_journal();
2820 return;
2821 }
2822
2823 u = manager_get_unit(m, SPECIAL_JOURNALD_SERVICE"systemd-journald.service");
2824 if (u && SERVICE(u)->state != SERVICE_RUNNING) {
2825 log_close_journal();
2826 return;
2827 }
2828
2829 /* Hmm, OK, so the socket is fully up and the service is up
2830 * too, then let's make use of the thing. */
2831 log_open();
2832}

2852static bool_Bool manager_get_show_status(Manager *m, StatusType type) {
2853 assert(m)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(m)),0))) log_assert_failed("m"
, "src/core/manager.c", 2853, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (
0);
2854
2855 if (!MANAGER_IS_SYSTEM(m)((m)->unit_file_scope == UNIT_FILE_SYSTEM))
2856 return false0;
2857
2858 if (m->no_console_output)
2859 return false0;
2860
2861 if (!IN_SET(manager_state(m), MANAGER_INITIALIZING, MANAGER_STARTING, MANAGER_STOPPING)({ _Bool _found = 0; static __attribute__ ((unused)) char _static_assert__macros_need_to_be_extended
[20 - sizeof((int[]){MANAGER_INITIALIZING, MANAGER_STARTING, MANAGER_STOPPING
})/sizeof(int)]; switch(manager_state(m)) { case MANAGER_INITIALIZING
: case MANAGER_STARTING: case MANAGER_STOPPING: _found = 1; break
; default: break; } _found; }))
2862 return false0;
2863
2864 /* If we cannot find out the status properly, just proceed. */
2865 if (type != STATUS_TYPE_EMERGENCY && manager_check_ask_password(m) > 0)
2866 return false0;
2867
2868 if (m->show_status > 0)
2869 return true1;
2870
2871 return false0;
2872}

2874void manager_set_first_boot(Manager *m, bool_Bool b) {
2875 assert(m)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(m)),0))) log_assert_failed("m"
, "src/core/manager.c", 2875, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (
0);
2876
2877 if (!MANAGER_IS_SYSTEM(m)((m)->unit_file_scope == UNIT_FILE_SYSTEM))
2878 return;
2879
2880 if (m->first_boot != (int) b) {
2881 if (b)
2882 (void) touch("/run/systemd/first-boot");
2883 else
2884 (void) unlink("/run/systemd/first-boot");
2885 }
2886
2887 m->first_boot = b;
2888}
2889
2890void manager_status_printf(Manager *m, StatusType type, const char *status, const char *format, ...) {
2891 va_list ap;
2892
2893 /* If m is NULL, assume we're after shutdown and let the messages through. */
2894
2895 if (m && !manager_get_show_status(m, type))
2896 return;
2897
2898 /* XXX We should totally drop the check for ephemeral here
2899 * and thus effectively make 'Type=idle' pointless. */
2900 if (type == STATUS_TYPE_EPHEMERAL && m && m->n_on_console > 0)
2901 return;
2902
2903 va_start(ap, format)__builtin_va_start(ap, format);
2904 status_vprintf(status, true1, type == STATUS_TYPE_EPHEMERAL, format, ap);
2905 va_end(ap)__builtin_va_end(ap);
2906}

2928int manager_update_failed_units(Manager *m, Unit *u, bool_Bool failed) {
2929 unsigned size;
2930 int r;
2931
2932 assert(m)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(m)),0))) log_assert_failed("m"
, "src/core/manager.c", 2932, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (
0);
2933 assert(u->manager == m)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(u->manager == m)),0))) log_assert_failed
("u->manager == m", "src/core/manager.c", 2933, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__
); } while (0);
2934
2935 size = set_size(m->failed_units);
2936
2937 if (failed) {
2938 r = set_ensure_allocated(&m->failed_units, NULL)internal_set_ensure_allocated(&m->failed_units, ((void
*)0) );
2939 if (r < 0)
2940 return log_oom()log_oom_internal("src/core/manager.c", 2940, __func__);
2941
2942 if (set_put(m->failed_units, u) < 0)
2943 return log_oom()log_oom_internal("src/core/manager.c", 2943, __func__);
2944 } else
2945 (void) set_remove(m->failed_units, u);
2946
2947 if (set_size(m->failed_units) != size)
2948 bus_manager_send_change_signal(m);
2949
2950 return 0;
2951}
2952
2953ManagerState manager_state(Manager *m) {
2954 Unit *u;
2955
2956 assert(m)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(m)),0))) log_assert_failed("m"
, "src/core/manager.c", 2956, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__); } while (
0);
2957
2958 /* Did we ever finish booting? If not then we are still starting up */
2959 if (!dual_timestamp_is_set(&m->finish_timestamp)) {
2960
2961 u = manager_get_unit(m, SPECIAL_BASIC_TARGET"basic.target");
2962 if (!u || !UNIT_IS_ACTIVE_OR_RELOADING(unit_active_state(u)))
2963 return MANAGER_INITIALIZING;
2964
2965 return MANAGER_STARTING;
2966 }
2967
2968 /* Is the special shutdown target queued? If so, we are in shutdown state */
2969 u = manager_get_unit(m, SPECIAL_SHUTDOWN_TARGET"shutdown.target");
2970 if (u && u->job && IN_SET(u->job->type, JOB_START, JOB_RESTART, JOB_RELOAD_OR_START)({ _Bool _found = 0; static __attribute__ ((unused)) char _static_assert__macros_need_to_be_extended
[20 - sizeof((int[]){JOB_START, JOB_RESTART, JOB_RELOAD_OR_START
})/sizeof(int)]; switch(u->job->type) { case JOB_START:
case JOB_RESTART: case JOB_RELOAD_OR_START: _found = 1; break
; default: break; } _found; }))
2971 return MANAGER_STOPPING;
2972
2973 /* Are the rescue or emergency targets active or queued? If so we are in maintenance state */
2974 u = manager_get_unit(m, SPECIAL_RESCUE_TARGET"rescue.target");
2975 if (u && (UNIT_IS_ACTIVE_OR_ACTIVATING(unit_active_state(u)) ||
2976 (u->job && IN_SET(u->job->type, JOB_START, JOB_RESTART, JOB_RELOAD_OR_START)({ _Bool _found = 0; static __attribute__ ((unused)) char _static_assert__macros_need_to_be_extended
[20 - sizeof((int[]){JOB_START, JOB_RESTART, JOB_RELOAD_OR_START
})/sizeof(int)]; switch(u->job->type) { case JOB_START:
case JOB_RESTART: case JOB_RELOAD_OR_START: _found = 1; break
; default: break; } _found; }))))
2977 return MANAGER_MAINTENANCE;
2978
2979 u = manager_get_unit(m, SPECIAL_EMERGENCY_TARGET"emergency.target");
2980 if (u && (UNIT_IS_ACTIVE_OR_ACTIVATING(unit_active_state(u)) ||
2981 (u->job && IN_SET(u->job->type, JOB_START, JOB_RESTART, JOB_RELOAD_OR_START)({ _Bool _found = 0; static __attribute__ ((unused)) char _static_assert__macros_need_to_be_extended
[20 - sizeof((int[]){JOB_START, JOB_RESTART, JOB_RELOAD_OR_START
})/sizeof(int)]; switch(u->job->type) { case JOB_START:
case JOB_RESTART: case JOB_RELOAD_OR_START: _found = 1; break
; default: break; } _found; }))))
2982 return MANAGER_MAINTENANCE;
2983
2984 /* Are there any failed units? If so, we are in degraded mode */
2985 if (set_size(m->failed_units) > 0)
2986 return MANAGER_DEGRADED;
2987
2988 return MANAGER_RUNNING;
2989}
